\mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_ab057e1afb884d1e29ecc02ebc883a8f1}\label{imgui__main_8c_ab057e1afb884d1e29ecc02ebc883a8f1}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!Settings@{Settings}}
\index{Settings@{Settings}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Settings}{Settings}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_settings__}{Settings\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__main_8c_ab057e1afb884d1e29ecc02ebc883a8f1}{Settings}}}



Settings System. 

Rather than pollute the global namespace, we collect together all the global settings into a structure that stores them. This also allows us to create a complete copy of the settings for the purpose of restoring them if the user cancels out of the Settings Dialog.

Like all of our structs, it\textquotesingle{}s C99 compliant. \mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_ac5795a0e93d9740c0f6a44ea312402bc}\label{imgui__main_8c_ac5795a0e93d9740c0f6a44ea312402bc}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!UiObject@{UiObject}}
\index{UiObject@{UiObject}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{UiObject}{UiObject}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ui_object__}{Ui\+Object\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__main_8c_ac5795a0e93d9740c0f6a44ea312402bc}{Ui\+Object}}}



This covers the inbuilt designs\+: Dolphin, Snowflake and Heart. Covers Rotate, Scale and Point UI events. 

scale is how radii are stored if the object is a circle, or the semi-\/major and semi-\/minor axes if the object is an ellipse.

center perhaps should be the \char`\"{}anchor\char`\"{} instead which is the center for some objects and top left for rectangular objects.

Do angles need special storage? angle\+Ref, angle\+New

This chapter details how the source code achieves the design detailed in the previous chapter. For the low-\/level details, read the later chapters.

Dear Im\+Gui (CITATION NEEDED)\hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_autotoc_md3}{}\doxyparagraph{Geometry Objects}\label{imgui__main_8c_autotoc_md3}
At all times the Emb\+Pattern has all of the information about the pattern however, editing information like the rubber text labels needs to be stored during runtime. Also editing ghosts like when a rotate command is half executed.

To deal with this we have a generic object that can act as any other object that updates the associated pattern struct as changes as made.

Note that the editor state is seperate from this since that is per view, not per object.

Selecting is done via this interface. \mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_a459ace9a6c614fe41b7f08ba91bc6dd4}\label{imgui__main_8c_a459ace9a6c614fe41b7f08ba91bc6dd4}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!UndoHistory@{UndoHistory}}
\index{UndoHistory@{UndoHistory}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{UndoHistory}{UndoHistory}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_undo_history__}{Undo\+History\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__main_8c_a459ace9a6c614fe41b7f08ba91bc6dd4}{Undo\+History}}}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{todo__todo000002}{Todo}}]document this. \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_aaefa4a2326f0cd4b4f95198ad4926d40}\label{imgui__main_8c_aaefa4a2326f0cd4b4f95198ad4926d40}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!View@{View}}
\index{View@{View}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{View}{View}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_view__}{View\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_view}{View}}}

\hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_autotoc_md4}{}\doxysubsubsection{Views}\label{imgui__main_8c_autotoc_md4}
The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_view}{View}} describes how the render is displayed. 

\doxysubsubsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_a29bcbce98e36705fa9c1577a227d53c0}\label{imgui__main_8c_a29bcbce98e36705fa9c1577a227d53c0}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!OBJ\_KEYS@{OBJ\_KEYS}}
\index{OBJ\_KEYS@{OBJ\_KEYS}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{OBJ\_KEYS}{OBJ\_KEYS}}

\index{actuator@{actuator}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{actuator()}{actuator()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static void actuator (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char}]{command\+\_\+line\mbox{[}200\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



The unified user interaction system which operates like a command line parser. 

{\itshape command\+\_\+line} 

In order to have a complex version of saving work, with backups, undo history and forks we need a good recording of what has happened.

An action has been taken, we are at the current head of the stack.

The action string is command similar to how a command line works\+: seperated by spaces we have a function followed by arguments.

\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{emb\_clamp()}{emb\_clamp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{embroidery_8h_a2082be9aabfb541dff1825c4ca6a05cd}{Emb\+Real}} emb\+\_\+clamp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{embroidery_8h_a2082be9aabfb541dff1825c4ca6a05cd}{Emb\+Real}}}]{lower,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{embroidery_8h_a2082be9aabfb541dff1825c4ca6a05cd}{Emb\+Real}}}]{x,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{embroidery_8h_a2082be9aabfb541dff1825c4ca6a05cd}{Emb\+Real}}}]{upper }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Ensure that x lies in the range \mbox{[}{\itshape lower}, {\itshape upper}\mbox{]} by rounding up or down if x is outside of that range. 

{\itshape lower} The minimum permittable value {\itshape x} can take. {\itshape x} The value to be processed. {\itshape upper} The maximum permittable value {\itshape x} can take. Returns Emb\+Real The clamped value.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_ab32b7623b4a8feb9ddb21f061a97217a}\label{imgui__main_8c_ab32b7623b4a8feb9ddb21f061a97217a}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!log\_debug@{log\_debug}}
\index{log\_debug@{log\_debug}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{log\_debug()}{log\_debug()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void log\+\_\+debug (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{msg }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Rather than outputting debug information to the command line it is sent to a file called \char`\"{}debug.\+txt\char`\"{} which is in the current directory. 

{\itshape msg} The message to be be written to the end of the debug file.

The benefits of always logging to file are\+: they are easily requested from users who need help and we can search the debug log using grep and other tool.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{todo__todo000077}{Todo}}]log current time and process id alongside all debug information. \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{roundToMultiple()}{roundToMultiple()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int round\+To\+Multiple (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{round\+Up,  }\item[{int}]{num\+To\+Round,  }\item[{int}]{multiple }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Rounds integers to multiples of another given integer. 

This is used by the rulers to scale appropriately.

{\itshape round\+Up} Whether to round up or down\+: 1 if up, 0 if down. {\itshape num\+To\+Round} Input to be rounded. {\itshape multiple} The number which must be a factor of the result. Returns int The multiple which is the closest to num\+To\+Round. \mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_aabe2efa6627dbff786aa942b4d28220f}\label{imgui__main_8c_aabe2efa6627dbff786aa942b4d28220f}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_aff183f464042b39eab77ce3fe5acc7e8}\label{imgui__main_8c_aff183f464042b39eab77ce3fe5acc7e8}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!run\_script@{run\_script}}
\index{run\_script@{run\_script}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{run\_script()}{run\_script()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int run\+\_\+script (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



A basic line-\/by-\/line script processor to allow for extensions to the program. 

{\itshape filename} The path of the script to run. Returns int Whether the script was successful.

Since the actuator uses command line style parsing, a script is just a text file with each line a compatible command.

It should be stressed that this has no control flow on purpose. We don\textquotesingle{}t want this to be hacked into a full scripting language that could cause havoc on the user\textquotesingle{}s system.

However, it may be useful to set and get variables and define macros\+: neither of these will allow for endless loops, stack overflow or other problems that third-\/party scripts could introduce. \begin{DoxyVerb}example.sh
------------------------------------------------------------------
# Save characters by defining functions.
# The syntax features
# Semi-colon ';' seperates out lines like in bash.
# The line ending is the end of the function, but the style
# is a shell function, so we need to write the end brace.

donut() { circle $1 $2 $3 $5 ; circle $1 $2 $4 $5 }

donut 10 20 20 black
donut 20 40 20 black
------------------------------------------------------------------
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_a15e6a0068cdc86e48cd1d317a26186ea}\label{imgui__main_8c_a15e6a0068cdc86e48cd1d317a26186ea}}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{todo__todo000209}{Todo}}]Before saving to a stitch only format, Embroidermodder needs to calculate the optimal path to minimize jump stitches. Also based upon which layer needs to be stitched first, the path to the next object needs to be hidden beneath fills that will come later. When finding the optimal path, we need to take into account the color of the thread, as we do not want to try to hide dark colored stitches beneath light colored fills.\end{DoxyRefDesc}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_a421e5f914841061096ef1977d1501b32}\label{imgui__main_8c_a421e5f914841061096ef1977d1501b32}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!streq@{streq}}
\index{streq@{streq}!imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{streq()}{streq()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool streq (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{s1,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{s2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Wrapper for the the standard strncmp that is aware of our 200 character string limit. 

{\itshape s1} The first string, usually the variable data. {\itshape s2} The second string, usually the contant to compare against. Returns true when the strings match for the first 200 chracters, for longer strings that match this far this is the wrong tool. \mbox{\Hypertarget{imgui__main_8c_a686ae88c89aff7188a565b2ab25be799}\label{imgui__main_8c_a686ae88c89aff7188a565b2ab25be799}} 
\index{imgui\_main.c@{imgui\_main.c}!stub\_implement@{stub\_implement}}
